Census data: aggregation queries

Testing DuckDB queries against our census tables — the same queries we’ll run in the frontend via DuckDB-WASM.

Part 1: Arrondissement-level demographics (census_population.parquet) Part 2: DA-level star schema (geo_da, census_demographics, census_economics, census_income)

library(duckdb)
Loading required package: DBI
con <- dbConnect(duckdb())

Part 1: Arrondissement-level demographics

Load the parquet file

parquet_path <- here::here("pipelines", "transform", "input", "census_population.parquet")
dbExecute(con, sprintf("CREATE VIEW pop AS SELECT * FROM '%s'", parquet_path))
[1] 0

Quick look at the data

3. Compare age distribution across districts

Which districts are youngest/oldest? Compute share of population under 15 and over 65.

dbGetQuery(con, "
  WITH totals AS (
    SELECT arrondissement, SUM(population) AS total
    FROM pop WHERE year = 2021 AND sex = 'total'
    GROUP BY arrondissement
  ),
  young AS (
    SELECT arrondissement, SUM(population) AS pop_young
    FROM pop
    WHERE year = 2021 AND sex = 'total'
      AND age_group IN ('0-4', '5-9', '10-14')
    GROUP BY arrondissement
  ),
  old AS (
    SELECT arrondissement, SUM(population) AS pop_old
    FROM pop
    WHERE year = 2021 AND sex = 'total'
      AND age_group IN ('65-69', '70-74', '75-79', '80-84', '85-89', '90-94', '95-99', '100+')
    GROUP BY arrondissement
  )
  SELECT t.arrondissement,
         t.total,
         ROUND(100.0 * y.pop_young / t.total, 1) AS pct_under_15,
         ROUND(100.0 * o.pop_old / t.total, 1) AS pct_over_65,
         ROUND(100.0 * (t.total - y.pop_young - o.pop_old) / t.total, 1) AS pct_working_age
  FROM totals t
  JOIN young y USING (arrondissement)
  JOIN old o USING (arrondissement)
  ORDER BY pct_over_65 DESC
")

4. Population change 2016 → 2021

Compare total population across census years for districts that have data in both.

dbGetQuery(con, "
  WITH by_year AS (
    SELECT arrondissement, year, SUM(population) AS total
    FROM pop
    WHERE sex = 'total'
    GROUP BY arrondissement, year
  )
  SELECT a.arrondissement,
         a.total AS pop_2016,
         b.total AS pop_2021,
         b.total - a.total AS change,
         ROUND(100.0 * (b.total - a.total) / a.total, 1) AS pct_change
  FROM by_year a
  JOIN by_year b ON a.arrondissement = b.arrondissement
  WHERE a.year = 2016 AND b.year = 2021
  ORDER BY pct_change DESC
")

5. Sex ratio by district (2021)

Male/female ratio — only for districts with male/female breakdown.

dbGetQuery(con, "
  WITH by_sex AS (
    SELECT arrondissement, sex, SUM(population) AS total
    FROM pop
    WHERE year = 2021 AND sex IN ('male', 'female')
    GROUP BY arrondissement, sex
  )
  SELECT m.arrondissement,
         m.total AS male,
         f.total AS female,
         ROUND(100.0 * m.total / (m.total + f.total), 1) AS pct_male
  FROM by_sex m
  JOIN by_sex f ON m.arrondissement = f.arrondissement
  WHERE m.sex = 'male' AND f.sex = 'female'
  ORDER BY pct_male DESC
")

6. Data coverage check

Which districts have male/female breakdown vs total-only? This matters for 2016 arrondissements (Ville de Montréal source = total only).

dbGetQuery(con, "
  SELECT year, source,
         COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN sex = 'male' THEN arrondissement END) AS has_sex_split,
         COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN sex = 'total' THEN arrondissement END) AS has_total,
         COUNT(DISTINCT arrondissement) AS all_districts
  FROM pop
  GROUP BY year, source
  ORDER BY year, source
")
  year                       source has_sex_split has_total all_districts
1 2016 StatCan 2016 Census profiles            15        15            15
2 2016            Ville de Montréal             0        19            19
3 2021 StatCan 2021 Census profiles            15        15            15
4 2021            Ville de Montréal            19        19            19

7. Dependency ratio

Classic demographic indicator: (population < 15 + population 65+) / population 15-64. Only meaningful with total population (not sex-split to avoid double-counting).

dbGetQuery(con, "
  WITH classified AS (
    SELECT arrondissement, year,
           CASE
             WHEN age_group IN ('0-4','5-9','10-14') THEN 'young'
             WHEN age_group IN ('65-69','70-74','75-79','80-84','85-89','90-94','95-99','100+') THEN 'old'
             ELSE 'working'
           END AS age_class,
           population
    FROM pop
    WHERE sex = 'total'
  )
  SELECT arrondissement, year,
         SUM(CASE WHEN age_class = 'young' THEN population ELSE 0 END) AS young,
         SUM(CASE WHEN age_class = 'working' THEN population ELSE 0 END) AS working,
         SUM(CASE WHEN age_class = 'old' THEN population ELSE 0 END) AS old,
         ROUND(100.0 * (
           SUM(CASE WHEN age_class IN ('young','old') THEN population ELSE 0 END)
         ) / NULLIF(SUM(CASE WHEN age_class = 'working' THEN population ELSE 0 END), 0), 1) AS dependency_ratio
  FROM classified
  GROUP BY arrondissement, year
  HAVING SUM(population) > 1000
  ORDER BY year, dependency_ratio DESC
")
                             arrondissement year young working   old
1                            Côte-Saint-Luc 2016  5655   17305  9485
2                                 Westmount 2016  3030   12030  5260

Part 2: DA-level star schema

The DA-level data uses a star schema: one geometry table (geo_da) joined with long-format fact tables. This is the architecture for the DuckDB-WASM frontend.

Load the star schema tables

dbExecute(con, "INSTALL spatial; LOAD spatial;")
[1] 0
load_dir <- here::here("pipelines", "load", "output")
dbExecute(con, sprintf("CREATE VIEW geo AS SELECT * FROM '%s/geo_da.parquet'", load_dir))
[1] 0
dbExecute(con, sprintf("CREATE VIEW demo AS SELECT * FROM '%s/census_demographics.parquet'", load_dir))
[1] 0
dbExecute(con, sprintf("CREATE VIEW econ AS SELECT * FROM '%s/census_economics.parquet'", load_dir))
[1] 0
dbExecute(con, sprintf("CREATE VIEW income AS SELECT * FROM '%s/census_income.parquet'", load_dir))
[1] 0

Table sizes

dbGetQuery(con, "
  SELECT 'geo_da' AS tbl, COUNT(*) AS rows FROM geo
  UNION ALL SELECT 'demographics', COUNT(*) FROM demo
  UNION ALL SELECT 'economics', COUNT(*) FROM econ
  UNION ALL SELECT 'income', COUNT(*) FROM income
")
           tbl   rows
1       geo_da   3219
2 demographics 204435
3    economics  94105
4       income 373175

9. Youngest and oldest DAs

Which DAs have the highest share of seniors (65+)?

dbGetQuery(con, "
  WITH totals AS (
    SELECT geo_uid, SUM(population) AS total
    FROM demo WHERE sex = 'total'
    GROUP BY geo_uid
    HAVING total > 100
  ),
  old AS (
    SELECT geo_uid, SUM(population) AS pop_65plus
    FROM demo
    WHERE sex = 'total'
      AND age_group IN ('65-69','70-74','75-79','80-84','85-89','90-94','95-99','100+')
    GROUP BY geo_uid
  )
  SELECT t.geo_uid,
         t.total,
         o.pop_65plus,
         ROUND(100.0 * o.pop_65plus / t.total, 1) AS pct_65plus
  FROM totals t JOIN old o USING (geo_uid)
  ORDER BY pct_65plus DESC
  LIMIT 15
")
    geo_uid total pop_65plus pct_65plus
1  24662595   470        440       93.6
2  24662821  1210       1030       85.1
3  24663400   520        440       84.6
4  24662819  1350       1135       84.1
5  24662658   575        480       83.5
6  24663271   640        510       79.7
7  24663277  2060       1555       75.5
8  24662705   535        400       74.8

14. Income inequality across DAs

Compute % earning over $100K from the bracket data.

dbGetQuery(con, "
  WITH brackets AS (
    SELECT geo_uid,
      SUM(count) AS total_pop,
      SUM(CASE WHEN bracket IN ('$100,000-$149,999', '$150,000+')
               THEN count ELSE 0 END) AS over_100k
    FROM income
    WHERE income_type = 'total_income' AND sex = 'total'
    GROUP BY geo_uid
    HAVING total_pop > 100
  )
  SELECT geo_uid, total_pop, over_100k,
         ROUND(100.0 * over_100k / total_pop, 1) AS pct_over_100k
  FROM brackets
  ORDER BY pct_over_100k DESC
  LIMIT 15
")
    geo_uid total_pop over_100k pct_over_100k
1  24660654       320       150          46.9
2  24661400       300       140          46.7
3  24661399       335       155          46.3
4  24660714       370       170          45.9
5  24661409       405       185          45.7
6  24660710       460       210          45.7
7  24661072       440       195          44.3

15. Join pattern: geo + economics

The fundamental frontend query — join geometry with a fact table for choropleths.

dbGetQuery(con, "
  SELECT g.geo_uid, g.area_sqkm, e.value AS median_income
  FROM geo g
  JOIN econ e ON g.geo_uid = e.geo_uid
  WHERE e.variable = 'median_income_household'
  ORDER BY e.value DESC
  LIMIT 10
")
    geo_uid area_sqkm median_income
1  24660710    0.5010        460000
2  24660713    0.1023        416000
3  24660714    0.1767        412000

16. Gender income gap by DA

Compare male vs female median income.

dbGetQuery(con, "
  WITH by_sex AS (
    SELECT geo_uid, sex, value
    FROM econ
    WHERE variable = 'median_income' AND sex IN ('male', 'female')
      AND value IS NOT NULL AND value > 0
  )
  SELECT m.geo_uid,
         m.value AS male_median,
         f.value AS female_median,
         ROUND(100.0 * (m.value - f.value) / m.value, 1) AS gap_pct
  FROM by_sex m
  JOIN by_sex f ON m.geo_uid = f.geo_uid
  WHERE m.sex = 'male' AND f.sex = 'female'
  ORDER BY gap_pct DESC
  LIMIT 15
")
    geo_uid male_median female_median gap_pct
1  24660758       56000         22200    60.4
2  24662508       71000         33200    53.2
3  24661948       50400         23800    52.8
4  24661282       24800         12300    50.4
5  24660169       61200         30600    50.0
6  24660386       49600         26400    46.8
7  24661310       29600         15900    46.3

17. Household income distribution comparison: renters vs owners

Cross-table query: join economics (tenure) with income brackets for DAs that are majority-renter vs majority-owner.

dbGetQuery(con, "
  WITH tenure AS (
    SELECT geo_uid,
      MAX(CASE WHEN variable = 'tenure_owner' THEN value END) AS owners,
      MAX(CASE WHEN variable = 'tenure_renter' THEN value END) AS renters
    FROM econ
    WHERE variable IN ('tenure_owner', 'tenure_renter')
    GROUP BY geo_uid
    HAVING owners > 0 AND renters > 0
  ),
  classified AS (
    SELECT geo_uid,
      CASE WHEN renters > owners THEN 'majority_renter' ELSE 'majority_owner' END AS tenure_type
    FROM tenure
  )
  SELECT c.tenure_type, i.bracket,
         SUM(i.count) AS total_count
  FROM classified c
  JOIN income i ON c.geo_uid = i.geo_uid
  WHERE i.income_type = 'household_total_income' AND i.sex = 'total'
  GROUP BY c.tenure_type, i.bracket
  ORDER BY c.tenure_type, i.bracket
")
       tenure_type           bracket total_count
